Secondly: The executive room you booked comes with executive benefits. The desserts at the happy hour in the evening are super delicious. There are many styles. The baking skills are really professional. I actually gave up the idea of ‚Äã‚Äãgoing out for food. The potato beef is very delicious and the small siomai is soft. Soft and glutinous, all kinds of fresh fruits, oh my god, my best friend always said it was so deliciousüòã! The key executive lounge faces the Ferris wheel, and the view can be given full marks. Such a good view and such delicious food!

Service: The hotel's service is extremely good, with five-star praise. Regardless of whether the check-in staff gave us welcome fruits or because we needed to delay check-out, the customer service lady‚Äôs thoughtfulness made it possible to postpone the check-out. A lady at the check-out concierge that night was very enthusiastic and helped carry our luggage to the car while we waited for the bus. Always helping to take care of the accompanying children, every detail is perfect.
The hotel's buffet is in the revolving restaurant on the top floor. The breakfast is very rich. The noodles are particularly delicious and there are many side dishes. You can eat them until the skin bursts. The female chef who cooks the noodles is very enthusiastic and will call you as soon as the noodles are cooked. He took the trouble to call guests to get noodles. This has never been seen in other five-star hotels. It is really so welcoming!
There is a pedestrian street one kilometer away from the hotel with a lot of delicious food. The night view from the hotel room is also amazing. The Ferris wheel is brilliant, the traffic is busy, and the stars are shining. I really think it is worth booking this hotel!
Finally, I would like to praise the service of Ctrip Hotel. After booking the hotel, the hotel temporarily adjusted the price due to availability of rooms, so there was a slight price difference. When I contacted Ctrip customer service, the housekeeper coordinated and made up the price difference immediately. They were very professional and timely. This is also the reason why I like to book a room on Ctrip. After the adjus**ent, the hotel staff contacted me as soon as possible and confirmed breakfast. When the children left, they said many times that they were reluctant to leave!
